### dist/module.json
```json
{"id":"sr5-marketplace","title":"Shadowrun 5e Marketplace","description":"A module to enhance the Shadowrun 5e system with a marketplace feature.","version":"#{VERSION}#","library":false,"compatibility":{"minimum":13,"verified":13,"maximum":13},"authors":[{"name":"Shadow","url":"https://github.com/shadows-eye/sr5-marketplace","discord":"shadows_plays"}],"relationships":{"systems":[{"id":"shadowrun5e","compatibility":{"minimum":"0.30.0"}}]},"socket":true,"styles":["styles/marketplace.css"],"esmodules":["scripts/marketHooks.js"],"languages":[{"lang":"en","name":"English","path":"languages/en.json"},{"lang":"de","name":"Deutsch","path":"languages/de.json"}],"documentTypes":{"Item":{"basket":{}},"Actor":{"shop":{}}},"url":"#{URL}#","manifest":"#{MANIFEST}#","download":"#{DOWNLOAD}#","license":"LICENSE","readme":"README.md","media":[{"type":"icon","url":"https://avatars2.githubusercontent.com/u/71292812?s=400&u=ccdb4eeb7abf551ca8f314e5a9bfd0479a4d3d41&v=4"}]}
```

### dist/scripts/marketHooks.js
```js
var e = class {
 async buildIndex() {
 let e = document.createElement("div");
 e.id = "sr5-marketplace-progress-container", Object.assign(e.style, {
 position: "fixed",
 top: "80px",
 left: "50%",
 transform: "translateX(-50%)",
 width: "90vw",
 maxWidth: "1200px",
 backgroundColor: "rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.8)",
 color: "white",
 padding: "10px",
 borderRadius: "5px",
 border: "1px solid #ff6400",
 boxShadow: "0 0 10px #000",
 zIndex: "10001",
 textAlign: "center"
 }), document.body.appendChild(e);
 let t = game.packs.filter((e) => e.metadata.type === "Item"), n = [...game.items.contents.filter((e) => !e.name.includes("#[CF_tempEntity]"))], r = 0;
 for (let i of t) {
 let a = await i.getDocuments();
 n.push(...a.filter((e) => !e.name.includes("#[CF_tempEntity]"))), r++;
 let o = Math.round(r / t.length * 100);
 e.innerHTML = `<span>Indexing: ${i.metadata.label} (${r}/${t.length})</span><progress value="${o}" max="100" style="width: 100%;"></progress>`;
 }
 let i = n.map((e) => {
 let t = e.toObject();
 return t.uuid = e.uuid, t;
 });
 return e.remove(), ui.notifications.info(game.i18n.localize("SR5Marketplace.Marketplace.Notifications.IndexComplete")), , i;
 }

function m(e) {
 let t = String(e ?? "").trim().match(/^(\d+)\s*([A-Za-z]*)$/);
 return {
 rating: t ? Number(t[1]) : 0,
 tag: t && t[2] ? t[2].toUpperCase() : ""
 };
}
var h = class {
 constructor() {
 this.testState = null;
 }
 static async getActor(e) {
 return e ? await fromUuid(e) : null;
 }
 static async getItem(e) {
 return e ? await fromUuid(e) : null;
 }
 async buildTestDialogContext(e, t = null) {
 if (this.testState = e, !this.testState) return null;
 switch (this.testState.status) {
 case "initial": return this.#e();
 case "result": return this.#t();
 case "extended-inprogress": return this.#n();
 case "resolved": return await this.#r(t);
 default: return console.error(`Unknown test status: "${this.testState.status}"`), null;
 }
 }
 async #e() {
 let { actorUuid: e, skill: t, attribute: n, connectionUuid: i, availabilityStr: a, appliedModifiers: o } = this.testState, s = await this.constructor.getActor(e);
 if (!s) return null;
 let c = [], l = 0, u = 0, d = s.system.skills.active[t];
 if (d) {
 let e = game.i18n.localize(CONFIG.SR5.activeSkills[t]);
 c.push({
 label: e,
 value: d.value
 }), l += d.value;
 }
 let f = s.system.attributes[n];
 if (f) {
 let e = game.i18n.localize(`FIELDS.attributes.${n}.label`);
 c.push({
 label: e,
 value: f.value
 }), l += f.value;
 }
 if (Array.isArray(o) && o.forEach((e) => {
 c.push({
 label: e.label,
 value: e.value
 }), l += e.value;
 }), i) {
 let e = await this.constructor.getItem(i);
 e && (u = e.system.connection, c.push({
 label: game.i18n.localize("SR5.Connection"),
 value: e.system.connection
 }), l += e.system.connection, c.push({
 label: game.i18n.localize("SR5.Loyalty"),
 value: e.system.loyalty
 }), l += e.system.loyalty);
 }
 return {
 actor: s,
 availabilityStr: a,
 modifierGroups: r.getModifiersForTest({ skill: t }),
 dicePoolBreakdown: c,
 totalDicePool: l,
 connectionUsed: u
 };
 }
 #t() {
 let e = this.testState.result, t = this.testState.rolls?.[0]?.terms[0]?.results || [], n = e.values.glitches.value, r = t.length, a = {
 diceResults: t,
 values: { glitches: { value: n } }
 };
 return {
 renderedDice: i.processDice(a),
 hits: e.values.hits.value,
 glitches: n,
 isGlitch: r > 0 ? n > r / 2 : !1
 };
 }
 #n() {
 let e = this.testState.result, t = this.testState.rolls, n = {
 diceResults: (t?.[t.length - 1])?.terms[0]?.results || [],
 values: { glitches: { value: e.values.glitches.value } }
 }, r = i.processDice(n);
 return {
 cumulativeHits: e.values.extendedHits.value,
 threshold: e.threshold.value,
 currentPool: e.pool.value,
 renderedDice: r
 };
 }
 async #r(e) {
 switch (this.testState.testType) {
 case "opposed": return this.#i();
 case "simple": return this.#a();
 case "extended": return await this.#o(e);

}, g = class {

 }

 r.createdForActor = t;

 }
 if (a === "stack" && o) o.buyQuantity += 1;
 else {
 let e = {
 basketItemUuid: "basket." + foundry.utils.randomID(),
 itemUuid: i.uuid,
 buyQuantity: 1,
 name: i.name,

 }
 }

 let n = t.flatMap((e) => Array(e.buyQuantity || 1).fill(e.availability));
 return e.totalAvailability = this._combineAvailabilities(n), e;

 F: 3,
 V: 3,
 R: 2,
 E: 2,
 "": 1
 }, n = 0, r = "";

 let a = parseInt(e[1] || "0", 10), o = (e[2] || "").toUpperCase();
 n += a, (t[o] || 0) > (t[r] || 0) && (r = o);
 }
 return `${n}${r}`;
 }

 }

 }

 static _walkObject(e, t, n, r = {}) {

 let a = t ? `${t}.${i}` : i, o = e[i], s = r[i] || this.#t(i);

async function z(e, t, ...n) {

 if (typeof r == "function") return await r.apply(e, n);
 if (r !== void 0) return r;
 let i = Object.getPrototypeOf(e);
 for (; i && i !== Object.prototype;) {
 let r = Object.getOwnPropertyDescriptor(i, t);
 if (r) {
 if (typeof r.value == "function") return await r.value.apply(e, n);
 if (typeof r.get == "function") return r.get.call(e);
 }
 i = Object.getPrototypeOf(i);
 }
 if (typeof e?.constructor?.[t] == "function") return await e.constructor[t](e, ...n);
 throw Error(`SR5 member "${t}" not found`);
}
var B = async (e) => typeof e == "string" ? await fromUuid(e) : e;
function V(e) {
 return ChatMessage.getSpeaker({ actor: e });
}

}
async function U(e, t) {

 return n && typeof n == "object" && (n = n.value ?? n.total ?? n.pool ?? 0), Number.isFinite(n) ? Math.max(0, n) : 0;
}
async function W(e, t) {
 let n = await z(e, "getSkill", t).catch(() => null);
 return Number(n?.value ?? n?.rating ?? n ?? 0);
}
function G(e) {

}
function K(e, t) {

 critGlitch: a && r === 0
 };
}
async function q(e) {

 return typeof t.evaluate == "function" ? await t.evaluate() : typeof t.evaluateSync == "function" && t.evaluateSync(), {

}

 actor: n.name,

 });

}
async function Y(e, t, { postToChat: n = !0 } = {}) {
 let r = await B(e), i = await B(t), o = G(r), s = [];

 key: e,

 net: l
 });
 }

}
async function X(e, t = [], { capByLeaderRating: n = !0, postToChat: r = !0 } = {}) {

 async updateSkillValue(e, t, n) {

 }

 }

 }

 };

 return t;
 }

 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("capitalize", function(e) {
 return typeof e != "string" || !e ? "" : e.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + e.slice(1);
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("hasKeys", function(e, t) {
 return e && Object.keys(e).length > 0 ? t.fn(this) : t.inverse(this);
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("for", function(e, t, n) {
 let r = "";
 for (let i = e; i < t; i += 1) r += n.fn(i);
 return r;
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("getTechnologyCost", function(e) {
 return e?.system?.technology?.cost || 0;
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("getKarma", function(e) {
 return e?.system?.karma || e?.flags?.sr5 - marketplace?.karma || 0;
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("getAvailability", function(e) {
 return e?.system?.technology?.availability || "Unknown";

 return e?.system?.essence || 0;
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("getField", function(e, t) {
 return e?.system?.[t] || "";
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("range", function(e, t, n) {
 let r = "";
 for (let i = e; i <= t; i++) r += n.fn(i);
 return r;
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("hasprop", function(e, t, n) {
 return e.hasOwnProperty(t) ? n.fn(this) : n.inverse(this);
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("ifin", function(e, t, n) {
 return t.includes(e) ? n.fn(this) : n.inverse(this);
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("ifgt", function(e, t, n) {
 return e > t ? n.fn(this) : n.inverse(this);
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("iflt", function(e, t, n) {
 return e < t ? n.fn(this) : n.inverse(this);
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("iflte", function(e, t, n) {
 return e <= t ? n.fn(this) : n.inverse(this);
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("ifne", function(e, t, n) {
 return e === t ? n.inverse(this) : n.fn(this);
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("ife", function(e, t, n) {
 return e === t ? n.fn(this) : n.inverse(this);
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("ift", function(e, t) {
 if (e) return t;
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("sum", function(e, t) {
 return e + t;
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("range", function(e, t, n) {
 let r = "";
 for (let i = e; i < t; i++) r += n.fn(i);
 return r;
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("ifeq", function(e, t, n) {
 return e === t ? n.fn(this) : n.inverse(this);
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("toLowerCase", function(e) {
 return e ? e.toLowerCase() : "";
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("eq", function(e, t) {
 return e === t;
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("neq", function(e, t) {
 return e !== t;
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("capitalizeFirst", function(e) {
 return typeof e != "string" || !e ? "" : e.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + e.slice(1);
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("jsonParse", function(e) {
 try {
 return JSON.parse(e);
 } catch {
 return console.error("Failed to parse JSON string in Handlebars:", e), {};
 }
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("isModifierActive", function(e, t) {
 return Array.isArray(t) ? t.some((t) => t.label === e) : !1;
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("loc", function(e, t) {
 return game.i18n.format(e, t.hash);
 }), Handlebars.registerHelper("invert", (e) => {
 if (typeof e != "object" || !e) return {};
 let t = {};

 return t;
```

```html
<div class="roll-dialog-container">

 {{!-- The clickable header. The 'for' attribute links it to the checkbox. --}}

 {{!-- The content that will be shown or hidden --}}
 <div class="collapsible-content">

 {{#each group.items as |mod|}}

 <div class="extended-test-summary">
 <span>Progress: <strong>{{activeTestState.cumulativeHits}} / {{activeTestState.threshold}}</strong> Hits</span>
 <span>Next Roll: <strong>{{activeTestState.currentPool}}</strong> Dice</span>
 </div>
 <div class="result-subtitle">Last Roll's Results:</div>
 <div class="MarketAppDialog-dice-tray">
 {{#each activeTestState.renderedDice as |die|}}
 <div class="MarketAppDialog-die-result {{die.cssClass}}">
 <span class="MarketAppDialog-die-text">{{die.text}}</span>
 </div>
 {{/each}}
 </div>
 <button type="button" class="roll-button" data-action="continueExtendedTest" data-dialog-id="{{activeTestState.id}}">
 Continue Test
 </button>
 </div>
 {{else if (eq activeTestState.status "resolved")}}
 <div class="MarketAppDialog-final-result-container">
 <details class="MarketAppDialog-final-summary" open>
 <summary>
 {{!-- This summary works for all test types --}}
 {{#if activeTestState.isAvailable}}
 <h3 class="success"><i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> {{localize "SR5Marketplace.Marketplace.Acquisition.Success"}}</h3>
 {{else}}
 <h3 class="failure"><i class="fas fa-times-circle"></i> {{localize "SR5Marketplace.Marketplace.Acquisition.Failed"}}</h3>
 {{/if}}
 </summary>
 {{!-- This block ONLY appears for a SUCCESSFUL EXTENDED test --}}
 {{#if (and activeTestState.isAvailable (eq activeTestState.testType "extended"))}}
 <div class="acquisition-details">
 <div class="detail-item">
 {{loc "SR5Marketplace.AppDialogItem.ExtendedSuccessDetails" 
 rolls=activeTestState.totalRolls 
 connection=activeTestState.connectionUsed 
 timeValue=activeTestState.deliveryTime.value 
 }} {{activeTestState.deliveryTime.unit}}
 </div>
 </div>
 {{/if}}
 {{!-- Check the test type to render the correct dice display grid --}}
 {{#if (eq activeTestState.testType "opposed")}}
 <div class="final-result-grid">
 <div class="result-column">
 <div class="result-title">{{localize "SR5Marketplace.AppDialogItem.YourRoll"}} ({{activeTestState.initialRoll.netHits}} {{localize "SR5Marketplace.AppDialogItem.netHits"}})</div>
 <div class="MarketAppDialog-dice-tray">
 {{#each activeTestState.initialRoll.renderedDice as |die|}}
 <div class="MarketAppDialog-die-result {{die.cssClass}}"><span class="MarketAppDialog-die-text">{{die.text}}</span></div>
 {{/each}}
 </div>
 </div>
 <div class="result-column">
 <div class="result-title">{{localize "SR5Marketplace.AppDialogItem.Resistance"}} ({{activeTestState.resistRoll.hits}} {{localize "SR5Marketplace.AppDialogItem.Hits"}})</div>
 <div class="MarketAppDialog-dice-tray">
 {{#each activeTestState.resistRoll.renderedDice as |die|}}
 <div class="MarketAppDialog-die-result {{die.cssClass}}"><span class="MarketAppDialog-die-text">{{die.text}}</span></div>
 {{/each}}
 </div>
 </div>
 </div>
 {{else}}
 {{!-- SIMPLE / EXTENDED TEST GRID --}}
 <div class="final-result-grid">
 <div class="result-column">
 <div class="result-title">{{localize "SR5Marketplace.AppDialogItem.FinalRoll"}} ({{activeTestState.netHits}} {{localize "SR5Marketplace.AppDialogItem.netHits"}})</div>
 <div class="MarketAppDialog-dice-tray">
 {{#each activeTestState.renderedDice as |die|}}
 <div class="MarketAppDialog-die-result {{die.cssClass}}"><span class="MarketAppDialog-die-text">{{die.text}}</span></div>
 {{/each}}
 </div>
 </div>
 <div class="result-column">
 <div class="result-title">{{localize "SR5.Threshold"}}</div>
 <div class="threshold-display">
 {{activeTestState.cumulativeHits}} / {{activeTestState.threshold}}
 </div>
 </div>
 </div>
 {{/if}}
 </details>
 </div>
 {{/if}}
 {{else}}
 <button type="button" data-action="showAvailabilityDialog" data-basket-uuid="{{basket.basketUUID}}">
 <i class="fas fa-dice-d6"></i> {{localize "SR5Marketplace.AppDialogItem.OrderTest"}}
 </button>
 {{/if}}
 </div>
</div>
```

```html
 <div class="stat-block">
 <label>{{localize "SR5.DamageValueAbbr"}}</label>
 {{#if isEditingBaseItem}}
 <input type="text" name="system.damage.value" value="{{displayItem.system.damage.value}}" class="item-input"/> 
 {{else}}
 <span>{{displayItem.system.damage.value}}</span>
 {{/if}}
 </div>
 <div class="stat-block">
 <label>{{localize "SR5.AccuracyAbbr"}}</label>
 {{#if isEditingBaseItem}}
 <input type="text" name="system.accuracy.value" value="{{displayItem.system.accuracy.value}}" class="item-input"/> 
 {{else}}
 <span>{{displayItem.system.accuracy.value}}</span>
 {{/if}}
 </div>
 <div class="stat-block">
 <label>{{localize "SR5.APAbbr"}}</label>
 {{#if isEditingBaseItem}}
 <input type="text" name="system.ap.value" value="{{displayItem.system.ap.value}}" class="item-input"/> 
 {{else}}
 <span>{{displayItem.system.ap.value}}</span>
 {{/if}}
 </div>
 {{/if}}
 {{!-- For Armor --}}
 {{#if (eq displayItem.type "armor")}}
 <div class="stat-block">
 <label>{{localize "SR5.Armor"}}</label>
 {{#if isEditingBaseItem}}
 <input type="text" name="system.armor.value" value="{{displayItem.system.armor.value}}" class="item-input"/> 
 {{else}}
 <span>{{displayItem.system.armor.value}}</span>
 {{/if}}
 </div>
 {{/if}}
 {{!-- Common stats --}}
 <div class="stat-block">
 <label>{{localize "SR5.Rating"}}</label>
 {{#if isEditingBaseItem}}
 <input type="text" name="system.technology.rating" value="{{displayItem.system.technology.rating}}" class="item-input"/> 
 {{else}}
 <span>{{displayItem.system.technology.rating}}</span>
 {{/if}}
 </div>
 <div class="stat-block">
 <label>{{localize "SR5.Availability"}}</label>
 {{#if isEditingBaseItem}}
 <input type="text" name="system.technology.availability" value="{{displayItem.system.technology.availability}}" class="item-input"/> 
 {{else}}
 <span>{{displayItem.system.technology.availability}}</span>
 {{/if}}
 </div>
 <div class="stat-block">
 <label>{{localize "SR5.Cost"}}</label>
 {{#if isEditingBaseItem}}
 <input type="text" name="system.technology.cost" value="{{displayItem.system.technology.cost}}" class="item-input"/>
 <i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-yen sr5-marketplace-yen details"></i> 
 {{else}}
 <span>{{displayItem.system.technology.cost}}</span>
 <i class="fa-duotone fa-solid fa-circle-yen sr5-marketplace-yen"></i>
 {{/if}}
 </div>
 {{#unless isEditingBaseItem}}
 {{#if (or builderData.baseItem.effects.length builderData.modifications.length)}}
 <div class="stat-block-divider"></div>
 {{/if}}
 {{#each builderData.baseItem.effects}}
 <div class="stat-block effect-stat">
 <label title="{{localize 'SR5Marketplace.ItemBuilder.Effects.InnateLockedHint'}}">
 <i class="fas fa-lock-alt"></i> {{this.name}}
 </label>
 <span>{{this.changes.[0].value}}</span>
 </div>
 {{/each}}
 {{#each builderData.modifications}}
 <div class="stat-block effect-stat custom-effect">
 <label title="{{localize 'SR5Marketplace.ItemBuilder.Effects.CustomEffect'}}">
 <i class="fas fa-bolt"></i> {{this.name}}
 </label>
 <span>{{this.changes.[0].value}}</span>
 </div>
 {{/each}}
 <div class="stat-block-divider"></div>
 <div class="stat-block description-block">
 <label>{{localize "SR5.Description"}}</label>
 <div class="description-content">{{{displayItem.system.description.value}}}</div>
 </div>
 {{/unless}}
 {{#if isEditingBaseItem}}
 <div class="stat-block-divider"></div>
 <div class="stat-block description-block">
 <label>{{localize "SR5.Description"}}</label>
 <textarea name="system.description.value" 
 rows="4">{{displayItem.system.description.value}}</textarea> 
 </div>
 {{/if}}
</div>
```

### dist/templates/apps/itemBuilder/partials/multi-select.html
```html
{{!-- 
 Reusable Multi-Select "Tagify" Component
 @param {string} name - The name attribute for the form data (e.g., 'system.selection_skills').
 @param {Array<object>} options - The list of all available options. Each object should have 'value' and 'label'.
 @param {Array<string>} selected - An array of the currently selected values.
 @param {string} placeholder - The placeholder text to show when no items are selected.
--}}
<div class="multi-select-container" data-name="{{name}}">
 <div class="tags-input" data-action="toggleMultiSelectDropdown">
 {{!-- The 'selected' variable is now an array of objects {id, value} --}}
 {{#each selected}}
 <span class="multi-select__tag" data-value="{{this.id}}">
 {{!-- Display the 'value' (label) from the object --}}
 {{this.value}}
 {{!-- The remove button uses the 'id' for its data-value --}}
 <i class="fas fa-times multi-select__tag-close" data-action="updateMultiSelect" data-value="{{this.id}}" data-mode="remove"></i>
 </span>
 {{/each}}
 <input type="text" class="multi-select__input" placeholder="{{#if selected}}{{else}}{{placeholder}}{{/if}}">
 </div>
 <div class="dropdown-content">
 {{#each options}}
 {{!-- Use our new 'isIdIn' helper to check against the array of objects --}}
 {{#unless (isIdIn ../selected this.value)}}
 <div class="dropdown-item" data-action="updateMultiSelect" data-value="{{this.value}}" data-mode="add">
 {{this.label}}
 </div>
 {{/unless}}
 {{/each}}
 </div>
</div>
```

```html
 <div class="skill-rating">{{skill.value}}</div>
 {{/if}}
 {{/each}}
 </div>
 </div>
 </div>
 </div>
 {{/each}}
 {{!-- Language Skills --}}
 <div class="collapsible-section">
 <input type="checkbox" id="toggle-language-skills" class="toggle">
 {{!-- FIXED: Changed <div> to <label> --}}
 <label class="sr5-marketplace" for="toggle-language-skills" class="toggle-label">
 <div class="marketplace-collapsible-header">{{localize "SR5Marketplace.Languages"}}</div>
 </label>
 <div class="toggle-content">
 <div class="language-skills skill-group">
 <div class="skill-header sr5-grid-3c">
 <span></span><span class="skill-name">{{localize "SR5Marketplace.Name"}}</span><span class="skill-rating">{{localize "SR5Marketplace.Rating"}}</span>
 </div>
 <div class="sr5-grid-3c">
 {{#each languageSkills as |skill|}}
 <div class="skill-icon" data-id="{{skill.id}}"></div>
 <div class="skill-name" data-id="{{skill.id}}">{{skill.name}}</div>
 {{#if @root.isEditMode}}
 <input class="value-input" type="number" name="system.skills.language.value.{{skill.id}}.value" value="{{skill.value}}"/>
 {{else}}
 <div class="skill-rating">{{skill.value}}</div>
 {{/if}}
 {{/each}}
 </div>
 </div>
 </div>
 </div>
</div>
```

```html
 <div class="item-cost">
 {{#if this.system.karma}}{{this.system.karma}}{{else}}{{this.flags.sr5-marketplace.Karma}}{{/if}}

 </div>

 <div class="item-rating">{{localize "SR5Marketplace.Marketplace.system.technology.rating"}}: {{this.system.technology.rating}}</div>
 {{#if (eq this.system.type "weapon")}}
 <div class="item-mod-detail">{{localize "SR5Marketplace.Marketplace.system.mount-point"}}: {{this.system.mount_point}}</div>
 {{/if}}
 {{#if (or (eq this.system.type "vehicle") (eq this.system.type "drone"))}}
 <div class="item-mod-detail">{{localize "SR5Marketplace.Marketplace.system.slots"}}: {{this.system.slots}}</div>
 {{/if}}
 {{else}}
 {{!-- This block is now restored to your preferred structure --}}
 {{#if (eq this.type "spell")}}
 <div class="item-drain">{{localize "SR5Marketplace.Marketplace.system.spell.drain"}}: {{this.system.drain}}</div>
 {{else if (eq this.type "quality")}}
 {{else if (eq this.type "adept_power")}}
 {{else if (eq this.type "complex_form")}}
 {{else if (eq this.type "metamagic")}}
 {{else if (eq this.type "echo")}}
 {{else}}
 <div class="item-all">{{localize "SR5Marketplace.Marketplace.system.avail.avail"}}: {{this.system.technology.availability}}</div>
 <div class="item-rating">{{localize "SR5Marketplace.Marketplace.system.technology.rating"}}: {{this.system.technology.rating}}</div>
 {{/if}}
 {{/if}}
 {{#if (or (eq this.type "bioware") (eq this.type "cyberware"))}}
 <div class="item-essence">{{localize "SR5Marketplace.Marketplace.system.essence"}}: {{this.system.essence}}</div>
 {{/if}}
 </div>
</div>
{{/each}}
```

```html
 </div>

 {{!-- The name must be 'test.data.limit' for the override to work --}}

 </div>
```
